             <a class="block__projects__item__title" href="/en/project/local-access-networks-can-unconnected-connect-themselves">
              Local Access Networks: Can the unconnected connect themselves?
             </a>
             <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
              <span>
               31 August 2017
              </span>
             </span>
             <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
             </p>
             <p>
              This project aims to address the following questions: Are local access infrastructure models a viable alternative to connecting the unconnected, and if so, what are the circumstances that make them successful? What are the benefits to the local community in terms of well-being, gender equity and social or economic development where connectivity infrastructure is locally owned?
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="col-md-4">
            <div class="block__projects__item">

             </a>
             <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
              <span>
               22 March 2017
              </span>
             </span>
             <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
             </p>
             <p>
              AfriSIG, an initiative co-organised by APC and NEPAD, is a multistakeholder training initiative that aims to give Africans from diverse sectors and stakeholder groups the opportunity to gain knowledge and confidence to participate effectively in internet governance processes and debates.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>

             </a>
             <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
              <span>
               25 April 2016
              </span>
             </span>
             <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
             </p>
             <p>
              Building on a strong pre-existing coalition, this project will strengthen the participation of an already participating country (India, with active network member Point of View), and bring in new actors from two new countries: Sri Lanka, with Women and Media Collective, and Nepal, with LOOM.
             </p>

            <a class="block__apc_blog__item__title" href="/en/blog/online-gender-based-violence-palestine-means-losing-out-womens-participation">
             Online gender-based violence in Palestine means losing out on women's participation
            </a>
            <span class="block__apc_blog__item__meta">
             <span>
              22 June 2018
             </span>
             <strong>
              7amleh  Arab Center for Social Media Advancement for GenderIT.org
             </strong>
            </span>
            <p class="block__apc_blog__item__excerpt">
             In recent times there has been a dramatic increase in the use of internet and social media by Palestinians. In this context there is also a rising wave of online gender-based violence that leads to intimidation of women and self-censorship, which means that often women are withdrawing from social media platforms.
            </p>

             The international perspective of connecting the unconnected
            </a>
            <span class="block__apc_blog__item__meta">
             <strong>
              Mexico
             </strong>
             <span>
              19 June 2018
             </span>
             <strong>
              Karla Velasco Ramos
             </strong>
            </span>
            <p class="block__apc_blog__item__excerpt">
             You are probably reading this right now either from your phone, tablet or laptop, with an average speed of 2 Mbps, and you most likely feel frustrated every time you cannot load a webpage. Trust me, I can relate.But what would you do if I told you that you are part of the 47% of people that are privileged enough to be online and that there are still 3.9 billion people who lack internet access?

      <section class="block block-block columns-apc container clearfix" id="block-block-21">
       <h4 class="block-title">
        Columns
       </h4>
       <div class="left">
        <div class="photo">
         <img src="/sites/default/files/images/david-souter.jpg"/>
        </div>
        <p>
         <a href="/en/column/inside-information-society">
          Inside the Information Society
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         David Souter writes a weekly column for APC, looking at different aspects of the information society, development and rights. Davids pieces take a fresh look at many of the issues that concern APC and its members, with the aim of provoking discussion and debate. Issues covered include internet governance and sustainable development, human rights and the environment, policy, practice and the use of ICTs by individuals and communities.
        </p>
       </div>
       <div class="right">
        <div class="photo">
         <img src="/sites/default/files/images/jenni-radloff.jpg"/>
        </div>
        <p>
         <a href="/en/column/history-internet-and-apc">
          The internet of memory: Stories from the APC community
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         What were information and communication technologies like in the 1980s and 1990s? What are the stories of the genesis and evolution of non-profit computer networks working for social change? Twice a month, this section will take a historical look at the APC community's journey of internet activism and make links to where we are now. Join Jennifer Radloff in this retrospective trip exploring the connections between the past and the present.
        </p>
       </div>
      </section>

     var map = L.map('mapid', {
         center: [10.0, 5.0],
         minZoom: 2,
         zoom: 2
     });
     map.scrollWheelZoom.disable();
     map.zoomControl.setPosition('topright');
 
     L.tileLayer('http://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {}).addTo(map);
 
 
     var orgIcon = L.icon({
         iconUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Organisation.png',
         iconRetinaUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Organisation.png',
         iconSize: [21, 22],
         iconAnchor: [10, 22],
         popupAnchor: [10, 32]
     });
     var indIcon = L.icon({
         iconUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Individual.png',
         iconRetinaUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Individual.png',
         iconSize: [21, 31],
         iconAnchor: [10, 31],
         popupAnchor: [10, 41]
     });
 
     var markerClusters = L.markerClusterGroup();
 
     for (var i = 0; i < markers.length; ++i) {
         markers[i].locality = (!markers[i].locality) ? '' : markers[i].locality;
         var popup = '<div class="leaflet-popup-' + ((markers[i].organisation) ? 'organisation' : 'individual') + '-content">' +
             '<h1><a href="' + markers[i].url + '">' + markers[i].name + '</a></h1>' +
             '<div class="locality">' + markers[i].locality + '</div>' +
             '<div class="organisation-name"></div></div>';
 
         var icon = (markers[i].organisation) ? orgIcon : indIcon;
 
         var customOptions =
         {
             'maxWidth': '500',
             'className': 'custom'
         }
         var m = L.marker([markers[i].lat, markers[i].lng], {icon: icon}).bindPopup(popup, customOptions);
 
         markerClusters.addLayer(m);
     }
 
     map.addLayer(markerClusters);
 
 
     function redrawMapMarkers(orgs, inds) {
         markerClusters.clearLayers();
 
         for (var i = 0; i < markers.length; ++i) {
             if ((markers[i].organisation && orgs) || (!markers[i].organisation && inds)) {
                 markers[i].locality = (!markers[i].locality) ? '' : markers[i].locality;
                 var popup = '<div class="leaflet-popup-' + ((markers[i].organisation) ? 'organisation' : 'individual') + '-content">' +
                     '<h1><a href="' + markers[i].url + '">' + markers[i].name + '</a></h1>' +
                     '<div class="locality">' + markers[i].locality + '</div>' +
                     '<div class="organisation-name"></div></div>';
 
                 var icon = (markers[i].organisation) ? orgIcon : indIcon;
 
                 var m = L.marker([markers[i].lat, markers[i].lng], {icon: icon}).bindPopup(popup, customOptions);
 
                 markerClusters.addLayer(m);
             }
         }
     }
